Use a defined RPC base type; in the case of <strong>int</strong>, add size specifiers like <a href="small.md"><strong>small</strong></a>, <a href="short.md"><strong>short</strong></a>, or <a href="long.md"><strong>long</strong></a> to qualify the <strong>int</strong>.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1652"><dt><span id="internal_compiler_inconsistency_detected__the_type_offset_is_invalid._See_the_documentation_for_more_information."></span><span id="internal_compiler_inconsistency_detected__the_type_offset_is_invalid._see_the_documentation_for_more_information."></span><span id="INTERNAL_COMPILER_INCONSISTENCY_DETECTED__THE_TYPE_OFFSET_IS_INVALID._SEE_THE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_MORE_INFORMATION."></span>incohérence du compilateur interne détectée : le décalage de type n’est pas valide. échéant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1659">Specify your IDL files, ACF files, full MIDL command line, and diagnostic output, if any.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

<td><span id="MIDL2414"></span><span id="midl2414"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1669"><dt><strong>MIDL2414</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1669"><dt><strong>MIDL2414</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1670"><dt><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-Oicf__using_-OI"></span><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-oicf__using_-oi"></span><span id="FLOATING_POINT_OR_COMPLEX_RETURN_TYPES_WITH__DECODE__ARE_NOT_SUPPORTED_IN_-OICF__USING_-OI"></span>les types de retour à virgule flottante ou complexe avec [Decode] ne sont pas pris en charge dans-Oicf, à l’aide de-OI</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1670"><dt><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-Oicf__using_-OI"></span><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-oicf__using_-oi"></span><span id="FLOATING_POINT_OR_COMPLEX_RETURN_TYPES_WITH__DECODE__ARE_NOT_SUPPORTED_IN_-OICF__USING_-OI"></span>floating point or complex return types with [decode] are not supported in -Oicf, using -OI</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1671">Les procédures avec des types de retour à virgule flottante ou structure/Union ne sont pas prises en charge dans la sélection de style-Oicf.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1671">Procedures with floating point or structure/union return types are not supported in the -Oicf style pickling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1672">Une solution de contournement pour 32 bits consiste à utiliser le mode d’optimisation-OI lors de la sérialisation des données (à l’aide de [Encode] et/ou [Decode]).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1672">A work around for 32-bit is to use the -Oi optimization mode when serializing data (using [encode] and/or [decode]).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1673">Toutefois, comme l’interpréteur de style ancien et le support de prise en charge sont prêts à être déplacés après la sortie de Windows 2000, l’utilisation de pointeurs est fortement suggérée comme solution de contournement pour ce problème.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1673">However, as the old -Oi style interpreter and pickling support are slated to be phased out after the Windows 2000 release, using pointers is strongly suggested as the work around for this problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1674">Notez également que, en règle générale, la modification d’une méthode d’interface pour utiliser un pointeur [out, ref] au lieu de la valeur de retour provoquant le problème est entièrement compatible avec le câble et peut être facilement masquée à partir de la couche d’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1674">Also note that typically, changing an interface method to use an [out, ref] pointer instead of the return value causing the problem is fully backward-compatible on wire and can be easily hidden from the app layer.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1675">Cet avertissement peut être supprimé globalement en spécifiant-OI sur la ligne de commande MIDL ou pour une fonction individuelle en ajoutant l’attribut [optimize ( &quot; i &quot; )] à la fonction dans le fichier ACF.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1675">This warning can be suppressed globally by specifying -Oi on the MIDL command line or for an individual function by adding the [optimize(&quot;i&quot;)] attribute to the function in the ACF file.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1676">L’exemple suivant illustre le problème :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1676">The following example demonstrates the issue:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1677">Roo. idl :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1677">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>double GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="169a7-1678">Roo. ACF :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1678">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="169a7-1679">Une option permettant de contourner cette limitation consiste à passer un paramètre [out] pour conserver le résultat au lieu d’utiliser une valeur de retour :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1679">One option to work around this limitation would be to pass an [out] parameter to hold the result instead of using a return value:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1680">Roo. idl :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1680">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>void GetDouble([out] double *result); //top level pointer is a [ref] pointer</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="169a7-1681">Roo. ACF :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1681">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="169a7-1682">Comme nous l’avons vu précédemment, la solution décrite ci-dessus est correcte non seulement pour les nouvelles interfaces, mais également pour les solutions de contournement pour les anciennes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1682">As mentioned earlier, the solution described above is good not only for the new interfaces but also as a work-around for the old ones.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1683">La représentation filaire du nouvel &quot; argument out &quot; est la même que pour la valeur de retour (remarquez void comme nouvelle valeur de retour).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1683">The wire representation for the new &quot;out&quot; argument is the same as for the return value (notice void as the new return value).</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>
</tr>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1685"><dt><span id="the_return_type_is_not_supported_for_64-bit_when_using__decode_"></span><span id="THE_RETURN_TYPE_IS_NOT_SUPPORTED_FOR_64-BIT_WHEN_USING__DECODE_"></span>le type de retour n’est pas pris en charge pour 64 bits lors de l’utilisation de [Decode]</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1685"><dt><span id="the_return_type_is_not_supported_for_64-bit_when_using__decode_"></span><span id="THE_RETURN_TYPE_IS_NOT_SUPPORTED_FOR_64-BIT_WHEN_USING__DECODE_"></span>the return type is not supported for 64-bit when using [decode]</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1686">Les procédures avec des types de retour à virgule flottante ou structure/Union ne sont pas prises en charge en mode 64 bits lors de la sérialisation des données (à l’aide de [ <a href="encode.md"><strong>encode</strong></a>] et/ou [ <a href="decode.md"><strong>Decode</strong></a>]).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1686">Procedures with floating point or structure/union return types are not supported in 64-bit mode when performing data serialization (using [ <a href="encode.md"><strong>encode</strong></a>] and/or [ <a href="decode.md"><strong>decode</strong></a>]).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1687">Cela est lié à l’ancien interpréteur de style OI et le sérialiseur de données ne sont pas pris en charge sur la plateforme 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1687">This is related to the old style -Oi interpreter and data serializer not being supported on 64-bit platform.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1688">Pour plus d’informations, consultez la description de MIDL2414.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1688">Please see the description of MIDL2414 for more information.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1689">L’exemple suivant illustre cette erreur :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1689">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1690">Roo. idl :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1690">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>double GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="169a7-1691">Roo. ACF :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1691">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="169a7-1692">Voici une solution de contournement pour les interfaces nouvelles et anciennes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1692">The following is advised as a work-around for both new and old interfaces.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1693">Utilisez un paramètre [out] pour conserver le résultat au lieu d’utiliser une valeur de retour :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1693">Use an [out] parameter to hold the result instead of using a return value:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1694">Roo. idl :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1694">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>void GetDouble([out] double *result); //top level pointer is a [ref] pointer.</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="169a7-1695">Roo. ACF :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1695">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="169a7-1696">Notez que cette solution offre une compatibilité descendante complète sur câble, car la représentation filaire d’un pointeur [ref, out] ou d’un double est identique à celle d’un double.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1696">Note that this solution is fully backward-compatible on wire, as the wire representation of a [ref, out] pointer or a double is the same as that of a double.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1698"><dt><span id="transmitted_type_may_not_contain_a_full_pointer_for_either__wire_marshal__or__user_marshal_"></span><span id="TRANSMITTED_TYPE_MAY_NOT_CONTAIN_A_FULL_POINTER_FOR_EITHER__WIRE_MARSHAL__OR__USER_MARSHAL_"></span>le type transmis ne peut pas contenir un pointeur complet pour [wire_marshal] ou [user_marshal]</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1698"><dt><span id="transmitted_type_may_not_contain_a_full_pointer_for_either__wire_marshal__or__user_marshal_"></span><span id="TRANSMITTED_TYPE_MAY_NOT_CONTAIN_A_FULL_POINTER_FOR_EITHER__WIRE_MARSHAL__OR__USER_MARSHAL_"></span>transmitted type may not contain a full pointer for either [wire_marshal] or [user_marshal]</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1699">Les types avec les attributs [ <a href="wire-marshal.md"><strong>wire_marshal</strong></a>] ou [ <a href="user-marshal.md"><strong>user_marshal</strong></a>] ne peuvent pas contenir de pointeurs ([ <strong>ptr</strong>]) complets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1699">Types with [ <a href="wire-marshal.md"><strong>wire_marshal</strong></a>] or [ <a href="user-marshal.md"><strong>user_marshal</strong></a>] attributes may not contain full ([ <strong>ptr</strong>]) pointers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1700">Utilisez [ <a href="unique.md"><strong>unique</strong></a>] ou [ <a href="ref.md"><strong>ref</strong></a>] à la place.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1700">Use [ <a href="unique.md"><strong>unique</strong></a>] or [ <a href="ref.md"><strong>ref</strong></a>] instead.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1701">L’exemple suivant illustre cette erreur :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1701">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>typedef struct
{
    [ptr] long *a;    //Should use [ref] or [unique] instead
}
st1;
typedef [wire_marshal(st1)] struct
{
    long a;
}
st2:
void roo(st2 *s);    //MIDL2416</code></pre>
</dd> </dl></td>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1703"><dt><span id="transmitted_type_must_either_be_a_pointer_or_have_a_constant_size_for__wire_marshal__and__user_marshal_"></span><span id="TRANSMITTED_TYPE_MUST_EITHER_BE_A_POINTER_OR_HAVE_A_CONSTANT_SIZE_FOR__WIRE_MARSHAL__AND__USER_MARSHAL_"></span>le type transmis doit être un pointeur ou avoir une taille constante pour [wire_marshal] et [user_marshal]</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1703"><dt><span id="transmitted_type_must_either_be_a_pointer_or_have_a_constant_size_for__wire_marshal__and__user_marshal_"></span><span id="TRANSMITTED_TYPE_MUST_EITHER_BE_A_POINTER_OR_HAVE_A_CONSTANT_SIZE_FOR__WIRE_MARSHAL__AND__USER_MARSHAL_"></span>transmitted type must either be a pointer or have a constant size for [wire_marshal] and [user_marshal]</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1704">Les types de niveau supérieur avec les attributs [ <a href="wire-marshal.md"><strong>wire_marshal</strong></a>] ou [ <a href="user-marshal.md"><strong>user_marshal</strong></a>] doivent avoir une taille bien définie au moment de la compilation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1704">Top-level types with [ <a href="wire-marshal.md"><strong>wire_marshal</strong></a>] or [ <a href="user-marshal.md"><strong>user_marshal</strong></a>] attributes must have a well-defined size at compile time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1705">Ils ne peuvent pas être ou contenir des tableaux conformes ou de taille variable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1705">They cannot be or contain conformant or varying-sized arrays.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1706">L’exemple suivant illustre cette erreur :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1706">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>typedef struct        //Type contains variable-sized array
{
    long s;
    [size_is(s)] char a[];
}
st1;
typedef [wire_marshal(st1)] struct
{
    long a;
}
st2;
void roo(st2 *s);        //MIDL2417</code></pre>
</dd> </dl></td>

<td><span id="MIDL2418"></span><span id="midl2418"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1707"><dt><strong>MIDL2418</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1707"><dt><strong>MIDL2418</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1715"><dt><span id="Structures_containing_conformant_arrays_must_be_passed_by_reference"></span><span id="structures_containing_conformant_arrays_must_be_passed_by_reference"></span><span id="STRUCTURES_CONTAINING_CONFORMANT_ARRAYS_MUST_BE_PASSED_BY_REFERENCE"></span>Les structures contenant des tableaux conformes doivent être passées par référence</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1715"><dt><span id="Structures_containing_conformant_arrays_must_be_passed_by_reference"></span><span id="structures_containing_conformant_arrays_must_be_passed_by_reference"></span><span id="STRUCTURES_CONTAINING_CONFORMANT_ARRAYS_MUST_BE_PASSED_BY_REFERENCE"></span>Structures containing conformant arrays must be passed by reference</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1716">Les paramètres de niveau supérieur dans RPC doivent avoir une taille bien définie au moment de la compilation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1716">Top level parameters in RPC must have a well-defined size at compile time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1717">Ils ne peuvent pas être, ni contenir des tableaux conformes ou de taille variable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1717">They cannot be, nor contain conformant or varying-sized array.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1718">En outre, les utilisateurs ne peuvent pas coder/décoder un type sans taille bien définie.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1718">In addition, users cannot encode/decode a type without well-defined size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1719">Les applications doivent passer une structure variable de type struct/conforme à une data-ttu-id="169a7-1720">L’exemple suivant illustre cette erreur :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1720">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>typedef struct        //Type contains variable-sized array
{
    long s;
    [size_is(s)] char a[];
}
st1;
void roo(st1 s);        //MIDL2465
 
on .acf file
typedef [encode,decode] st1; //MIDL2465</code></pre>
</dd> </dl></td>

<td><span id="MIDL9008"></span><span id="midl9008"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1721"><dt><strong>MIDL9008</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1721"><dt><strong>MIDL9008</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1722"><dt><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._See_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._see_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_INTERNAL_COMPILER_PROBLEM__SYSTEM_ERROR_CODE__-_THE_COMPILER_CANNOT_CONTINUE_FOR_AN_UNKNOWN_REASON._SEE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_A_WORKAROUND."></span> problème interne du compilateur <system error code> - le compilateur ne peut pas continuer pour une raison inconnue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1722"><dt><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._See_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._see_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_INTERNAL_COMPILER_PROBLEM__SYSTEM_ERROR_CODE__-_THE_COMPILER_CANNOT_CONTINUE_FOR_AN_UNKNOWN_REASON._SEE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_A_WORKAROUND."></span> internal compiler problem <system error code> - the compiler cannot continue for an unknown reason.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1723">Consultez la documentation pour obtenir une solution de contournement.</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1723">See documentation for a workaround.</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1724">Le compilateur n’a pas pu continuer et la cause de l’erreur est inconnue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1724">The compiler could not continue and the cause of the error is unknown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1725">Le numéro d’erreur hexadécimal est un identificateur d’erreur système.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1725">The hexadecimal error number is a system-error identifier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1726">La compilation a peut-être échoué en raison d’un problème externe, tel qu’une condition de mémoire insuffisante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1726">The compile may have failed because of an external problem, such as an out-of-memory condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1727">Dans ce cas, vous trouverez plus d’informations dans Winerror. h ou Ntstatus. h.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1727">In that case, you can find more information in Winerror.h or Ntstatus.h.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1728">Il existe deux situations qui génèrent généralement cette erreur :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1728">There are two situations that usually generate this error:</span></span><br/>
<ul>
<li><span data-ttu-id="169a7-1729">Le compilateur MIDL n’a pas pu effectuer la récupération après avoir détecté une erreur dans le fichier IDL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1729">The MIDL compiler failed to recover after detecting an error in the IDL file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1730">Si MIDL a retourné des messages d’erreur relatifs à votre fichier IDL, essayez de les corriger et de recompiler.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1730">If MIDL returned any error messages about your IDL file, try fixing them and recompiling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1731">S’il n’y a aucun message d’erreur, le compilateur peut avoir échoué avant de signaler une erreur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1731">If there are no error messages, the compiler may have failed before it could report an error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1732">Recherchez une erreur de syntaxe sur la ligne pour laquelle l’erreur interne du compilateur est signalée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1732">Look for a syntax error on the line for which the internal compiler error is reported.</span></span></li>
<li><span data-ttu-id="169a7-1733">Le compilateur MIDL n’a pas pu générer de code correct sous une option d’optimisation spécifiée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1733">The MIDL compiler could not generate correct code under a specified optimization option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1734">Essayez de modifier les modes de compilateur, de compiler en optimisation en mode mixte (/<a href="-os.md"><strong>OS</strong></a>) ou de supprimer toutes les optimisations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1734">Try changing compiler modes, compiling in mixed-mode optimization (/<a href="-os.md"><strong>Os</strong></a>), or removing all optimizations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1735">Ou recompilez à l’aide de l’indicateur/NO_FORMAT_OPT pour supprimer l’optimisation par défaut de MIDL des descripteurs de procédure et de type.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1735">Or, recompile using the /NO_FORMAT_OPT flag to suppress MIDL's default optimization of procedure and type descriptors.</span></span></li>
</ul>
<span data-ttu-id="169a7-1736">Parfois, cette erreur se produit même lorsque le fichier IDL est correct et qu’aucune option d’optimisation n’est utilisée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1736">Occasionally this error occurs even when the IDL file is correct and no optimization options are being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1737">Si c’est le cas, essayez de réécrire la section de code à proximité de l’endroit où l’erreur a été signalée en supprimant les modifications récentes, en simplifiant ou en réorganisant les types de données, en modifiant les prototypes, ou bien commencer à commenter des parties du fichier IDL pour localiser le code de problème.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1737">If this is the case, try rewriting the section of code in the vicinity of where the error was reported by removing any recent modifications, simplifying or rearranging data types, changing prototypes, or else begin to comment out portions of the IDL file to locate the problem code.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="169a7-1738">Si aucune de ces options ne fonctionne, ou si vous pensez que le problème peut être lié à un bogue dans Midl.exe, contactez Microsoft, en donnant tous les détails appropriés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="169a7-1738">If none of these options works, or if you think the problem may be related to a bug in Midl.exe, please notify Microsoft, giving all the relevant details.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>
</tr>
